<details class="recipe-item">
<summary><h2>1-Hour Soft and Buttery Dinner Rolls</h2></summary>

<p>Link to recipe <a href="https://www.gimmesomeoven.com/1-hour-soft-buttery-dinner-rolls/">here</a>.</p>

<dl>
<dt>Yield</dt>
<dd>15, 15 servings</dd>
<dt>Prep time</dt>
<dd>PT45M</dd>
<dt>Cook time</dt>
<dd>PT15M</dd>
<dt>Total time</dt>
<dd>PT60M</dd>
</dl>

<h3>Ingredients</h3>

<ul>
<li>1 cup water</li>
<li>2 tablespoons melted butter</li>
<li>1/2 cup milk</li>
<li>2 tablespoons honey</li>
<li>1 tablespoon active-dry yeast*</li>
<li>3 1/2 to 4 cups all-purpose flour</li>
<li>1 teaspoon fine sea salt</li>
<li>extra melted butter (for brushing on top)</li>
</ul>

<p>Directions are available at the linked source.</p>

</details>

<details class="recipe-item">
<summary><h2>Almond Cranberry Bread</h2></summary>

<p>Link to recipe <a href="https://www.healthyseasonalrecipes.com/cranberry-almond-quick-bread/">here</a>.</p>

<dl>
<dt>Yield</dt>
<dd>10, 10 slices</dd>
<dt>Prep time</dt>
<dd>PT25M</dd>
<dt>Cook time</dt>
<dd>PT50M</dd>
<dt>Total time</dt>
<dd>PT1H15M</dd>
</dl>

<h3>Ingredients</h3>

<ul>
<li>1 cup plus 2 tablespoons white whole-wheat flour</li>
<li>1 cup almond flour</li>
<li>1 tablespoon baking powder</li>
<li>½ teaspoon salt</li>
<li>2 eggs, yolks and whites separated</li>
<li>1/3 cup organic canola oil or avocado oil</li>
<li>2/3 cup maple sugar or coconut sugar</li>
<li>1/2 cup fat-free milk, lactose-free if desired</li>
<li>1 teaspoon vanilla</li>
<li>½ teaspoon almond extract</li>
<li>1 cup cranberries, roughly chopped in food processor</li>
<li>¼ cup sliced almonds</li>
<li>1 tablespoon turbinado sugar, optional</li>
</ul>

<p>Directions are available at the linked source.</p>

</details>

<details class="recipe-item">
<summary><h2>Almond Waffles with Cranberry Orange Honey Syrup</h2></summary>

<p>Link to recipe <a href="https://www.healthyseasonalrecipes.com/almond-waffles-with-cranberry-orange-honey-syrup/">here</a>.</p>

<dl>
<dt>Yield</dt>
<dd>4, 4 to 5, depending on waffle iron</dd>
<dt>Prep time</dt>
<dd>PT30M</dd>
<dt>Cook time</dt>
<dd>PT20M</dd>
<dt>Total time</dt>
<dd>PT30M</dd>
</dl>

<h3>Ingredients</h3>

<ul>
<li>¾ cup honey</li>
<li>¾ cup fresh or frozen cranberries</li>
<li>1 teaspoon orange zest</li>
<li>2 large eggs, yolks and whites separated</li>
<li>½ cup almond oil or organic canola oil</li>
<li>1/3 cup almond milk or milk</li>
<li>3 tablespoons sugar, divided</li>
<li>¾ teaspoon almond extract</li>
<li>3/4 cup white whole-wheat flour</li>
<li>½ cup all-purpose flour</li>
<li>3 tablespoons almond meal</li>
<li>2 teaspoons baking powder</li>
<li>½ teaspoon salt</li>
<li>5 tablespoons toasted almonds</li>
</ul>

<p>Directions are available at the linked source.</p>

<dl>
<dt>Yield</dt>
<dd>6, 6 servings</dd>
<dt>Prep time</dt>
<dd>PT10M</dd>
<dt>Cook time</dt>
<dd>PT30M</dd>
<dt>Total time</dt>
<dd>PT40M</dd>
</dl>

<h3>Ingredients</h3>

<ul>
<li>1 1/2 tbsp. olive oil</li>
<li>1 medium onion, diced</li>
<li>4 garlic cloves, monced</li>
<li>1 tbsp. chipotle peppers in adobo sauce, minced ((see notes))</li>
<li>1 tsp. cumin powder</li>
<li>30 oz. (2 cans) black beans, rinsed</li>
<li>16 oz. fresh of frozen corn kernels</li>
<li>12 oz. red lentils, rinsed</li>
<li>14.5 oz. (1 can) diced tomatoes</li>
<li>14.5 oz. (1 can) tomato sauce</li>
<li>4 cups vegetable broth</li>
<li>1/2 cup cilantro leaves, chopped</li>
<li>2 tbsp. lime juice</li>
<li>salt and pepper, to taste</li>
</ul>

<dl>

<dd>PT5M</dd>

<dd>PT30M</dd>
</dl>

<h3>Ingredients</h3>

<li>2 tablespoons extra-virgin olive oil, or to taste</li>
<li>1 tablespoon fresh lemon juice, or to taste</li>
<li>1 teaspoon ground sumac, or to taste</li>
<li>1 clove garlic, crushed (or more to taste)</li>
<li>kosher salt and freshly ground black pepper to taste</li>

</ul>

<dd>PT20M</dd>
</dl>

<ul>

<li>2 cups shredded carrots</li>
<li>1 red bell pepper, (sliced into bite-sized pieces)</li>
<li>½ cup chopped fresh cilantro</li>
<li>3 tablespoons creamy peanut butter</li>
<li>3 tablespoons unseasoned rice vinegar</li>
<li>1 tablespoon fresh lime juice, (from one lime)</li>
<li>3 tablespoons vegetable oil</li>
<li>1 tablespoon soy sauce</li>
<li>3 tablespoons honey</li>
<li>1 tablespoon sugar</li>
<li>1 large clove garlic, (roughly chopped)</li>
<li>1-in square piece fresh ginger, (peeled and roughly chopped (see note))</li>
<li>¾ teaspoon salt</li>
<li>1 teaspoon sriracha</li>
<li>1 teaspoon sesame oil</li>
</ul>

<details class="recipe-item">
<summary><h2>Asian Slaw with Ginger Peanut Dressing</h2></summary>

<p>Link to recipe <a href="https://www.onceuponachef.com/recipes/asian-slaw-with-ginger-peanut-dressing.html">here</a>.</p>

<dl>
<dt>Yield</dt>
<dd>6, 6 as a side dish</dd>
</dl>

<h3>Ingredients</h3>

<ul>
<li>¼ cup honey</li>
<li>¼ cup vegetable oil</li>
<li>¼ cup unseasoned rice vinegar</li>
<li>1 tablespoon soy sauce</li>
<li>1 teaspoon sesame oil</li>
<li>1 tablespoon peanut butter ((I like Skippy Natural No Need to Stir))</li>
<li>Heaping ½ teaspoon salt</li>
<li>1 teaspoon Sriracha sauce ((optional))</li>
<li>1 tablespoon minced fresh ginger ((see note))</li>
<li>1 large garlic clove, (minced)</li>
<li>4 cups prepared shredded coleslaw</li>
<li>2 cups prepared shredded carrots</li>
<li>1 red bell pepper, (thinly sliced into bite-sized pieces)</li>
<li>1 cup cooked and shelled edamame</li>
<li>2 medium scallions, (thinly sliced)</li>
<li>½ cup chopped salted peanuts ((or you can leave them whole))</li>
<li>½ cup loosely packed chopped fresh cilantro</li>
</ul>

<p>Directions are available at the linked source.</p>

</details>

<dl>
<dt>Yield</dt>
<dd>About 1¼ cups</dd>

<dl>
<dt>Yield</dt>
<dd>4, 4 servings</dd>
<dt>Prep time</dt>
<dd>PT20M</dd>
<dt>Cook time</dt>
<dd>PT30M</dd>
<dt>Total time</dt>
<dd>PT50M</dd>
</dl>

<h3>Ingredients</h3>

<ul>
<li>1 tablespoon olive oil</li>
<li>1 onion (diced)</li>
<li>3 carrots (peeled and diced)</li>
<li>2 ribs celery (diced)</li>
<li>3 cloves garlic (minced)</li>
<li>1 tablespoon freshly grated ginger</li>
<li>1 tablespoon minced lemongrass</li>
<li>1 tablespoon chopped fresh thyme leaves</li>
<li>1 tablespoon chopped fresh rosemary</li>
<li>5 cups chicken stock</li>
<li>2 bay leaves</li>
<li>1 pound boneless, skinless chicken thighs</li>
<li>3/4 cup ditalini pasta</li>
<li>3 tablespoons freshly squeezed lemon juice</li>
<li>Kosher salt and freshly ground black pepper (to taste)</li>
<li>2 tablespoons chopped fresh chives</li>
</ul>

<p>Directions are available at the linked source.</p>

</ul>

</ul>

<li>2 medium ribs celery, (finely diced)</li>
<li>2 cloves garlic, (minced)</li>

<li>6 cups chicken broth</li>

<li>¼ teaspoon freshly ground black pepper</li>
<li>2 (15.5-oz) cans cannellini beans or chickpeas, drained and rinsed</li>
<li>¼ cup dried lentils, (rinsed (preferably French green lentils, but any green or brown lentils are fine))</li>
<li>1 (14.5-oz) can diced tomatoes, (with their juices)</li>
<li>2 bay leaves</li>
<li>1 tablespoon minced fresh rosemary</li>
<li>¾ cup pasta, (such as elbow macaroni or ditalini)</li>
<li>⅓ cup freshly grated Parmigiano-Reggiano, (plus more for serving)</li>
</ul>

<p>Directions are available at the linked source.</p>

<summary><h2>Shepherd’s Pie Recipe</h2></summary>

<p>Link to recipe <a href="https://www.thewholesomedish.com/the-best-classic-shepherds-pie/">here</a>.</p>

<dl>
<dt>Yield</dt>
<dd>6, 6 servings</dd>
<dt>Prep time</dt>
<dd>PT20M</dd>
<dt>Cook time</dt>
<dd>PT50M</dd>
<dt>Total time</dt>
<dd>PT70M</dd>
</dl>

<h3>Ingredients</h3>

<ul>
<li>2 tablespoons olive oil</li>
<li>1 cup chopped yellow onion</li>
<li>1 lb. 90% lean ground beef (-or ground lamb)</li>
<li>2 teaspoons dried parsley leaves</li>
